defined_text = {
    name = SMMGetColorScale
	random = no
    text = {
        localisation_key = SMMColorScaleReversed
        trigger = {
			has_country_flag = smm_rev
        }
    }
	text = {
		localisation_key = SMMColorScaleRegular
	}
}
defined_text = {
    name = SMMGetColorScaleRegular
	random = no
    text = {
        localisation_key = SMMColorScale_9
        trigger = {
			is_variable_equal = { which = smm_res value = 9 }
        }
    }
    text = {
        localisation_key = SMMColorScale_8
        trigger = {
			is_variable_equal = { which = smm_res value = 8 }
        }
    }
    text = {
        localisation_key = SMMColorScale_7
        trigger = {
        	is_variable_equal = { which = smm_res value = 7 }
        }
    }
    text = {
        localisation_key = SMMColorScale_6
        trigger = {
        	is_variable_equal = { which = smm_res value = 6 }
        }
    }
    text = {
        localisation_key = SMMColorScale_8
        trigger = {
			is_variable_equal = { which = smm_res value = 5 }
        }
    }
    text = {
        localisation_key = SMMColorScale_7
        trigger = {
			is_variable_equal = { which = smm_res value = 4 }
        }
    }
    text = {
        localisation_key = SMMColorScale_6
        trigger = {
			is_variable_equal = { which = smm_res value = 3 }
        }
    }
    text = {
        localisation_key = SMMColorScale_9
        trigger = {
			is_variable_equal = { which = smm_res value = 2 }
        }
    }
    text = {
        localisation_key = SMMColorScale_1
        trigger = {
			is_variable_equal = { which = smm_res value = 1 }
        }
    }
    text = {
        localisation_key = SMMColorScale_0
    }
}
